| <span data-ttu-id="afb06-842">Voce</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="afb06-842">Entry</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="afb06-843">Valore</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="afb06-843">Value</span></span> |
